It is possible for one gene to overlap with multiple segments, and in this case, copy_number, min_copy_number and max_copy_number could take different values. Origin: TEXT | blank about half the time, otherwise 'L' | eg=[" ", "L"]
PrevTum: TEXT | previous-tumor flag, either blank or 'Y' | eg=[" "]
SpecHerDis: TEXT | specific hereditary disease, eg 'Fanconi anemia' or 'inv(9)(p11q13)'

## PROD.MOLCLINABNORM
InvNo: NUMBER | investigation number, usually between 1 and 10 | eg=[1, 2]
OrderNo: NUMBER | order number, between 1 and 54 | eg=[1, 11]
RefNo: NUMBER | reference number, eg '15563' | eg=[1696, 4556]
Abnormality: TEXT | abnormality description, eg 't(19;19)(p13;p13)' or 'del(7)(q?)' | eg=["r", "+1"]
MolClin: TEXT | flag indicating molecular 'M', or clinical 'C' | eg=["C"]

## PROD.CYTOCONVERTED
Clone: NUMBER | NULL | eg=[1, 3]
Type: TEXT | NULL | eg=["Gain"]
End: NUMBER | NULL | eg=[50400000]
CellsPresent: TEXT | NULL | eg=["unknown"]
CaseNo: TEXT | NULL | eg=["56", "1"]
InvNo: NUMBER | NULL | eg=[1]
ChrOrd: NUMBER | NULL | eg=[14]
RefNo: NUMBER | NULL | eg=[12067, 5568]
Chr: TEXT | NULL | eg=["chr14"]
Start: NUMBER | NULL | eg=[0]

## PROD.CYTOBANDS_HG38
cytoband_name: TEXT | NULL | eg=["1p36", "1p34"]
hg38_stop: NUMBER | NULL | eg=[27600000, 46300000]
hg38_start: NUMBER | NULL | eg=[0, 34300000]
chromosome: TEXT | NULL | eg=["chr1"]
